<div id="review_2283727911" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2283727911" />
    <a title="Helena of Eretz ✰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27036454-helena-of-eretz"><img alt="Helena of Eretz ✰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596076376p2/27036454.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2283727911?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helena of Eretz ✰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helena of Eretz ✰" href="/user/show/27036454-helena-of-eretz">Helena of Eretz ✰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=hardback">hardback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2283727911&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2283727911" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11511829090513874083">Firstly, I’d like to slap myself in the face for waiting so long to continue on with this series. What the hell is wrong with me?!!! When I first read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16429619-the-kiss-of-deception' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Kiss of Deception</a> in 2014, I loved it, but I never read the following instalments in the Remnant Chronicles…and that has got to be the worst mistake I’ve EVER made (ok fine, not the “worst”, but still). I’m writing this review having just finished <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21569527-the-heart-of-betrayal' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Heart of Betrayal</a>, maybe 5 minutes ago, and I AM SO RAW WITH EMOTIONS. HOW COULD YOU DO THAT </span>
  <span id="freeText11511829090513874083" style="display:none">Firstly, I’d like to slap myself in the face for waiting so long to continue on with this series. What the hell is wrong with me?!!! When I first read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16429619-the-kiss-of-deception" rel="nofollow noopener">The Kiss of Deception</a> in 2014, I loved it, but I never read the following instalments in the Remnant Chronicles…and that has got to be the worst mistake I’ve EVER made (ok fine, not the “worst”, but still). I’m writing this review having just finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21569527-the-heart-of-betrayal" rel="nofollow noopener">The Heart of Betrayal</a>, maybe 5 minutes ago, and I AM SO RAW WITH EMOTIONS. HOW COULD YOU DO THAT TO ME, MARY E. PEARSON?!!! (P.S. I’m sorry, but this will be an incredibly fangirly review :P)<br><br>Needless to say, this book is being rated, not only a full-5 stars, but ALL THE STARS IN THE WORLD!!! I have absolutely no complaints with the writing, the plot (OMG THAT ENDING), the world building, or the character development. <b>A+</b>!!!<br><br>And I also need to take a moment to mourn my <i>beautiful baby, Aster</i>…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1525971640ra/25518547.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>MARY E. PEARSON, YOU MONSTER!!! She was so cute and innocent and pure and aghhhh!!! I was hoping that she’d be able to run off with Lia to safety, but then my hopes and dreams were completely crushed!<br><br>This was also a semi-buddy read with my fellow #TeamRafe shipper, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2396712488?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Diana</a>! :)<br><br><blockquote>
<br> <i>“There are no rules in survival.”</i><br>
</blockquote><br>So…where to begin? Let’s start with <b>Lia</b>. OMG, talk about character development!!! We already knew how protective and fierce she was…yet we also knew that she was somewhat flighty in the previous book, wanting to choose her own adventures and fall in love. However, in The Heart of Betrayal, we see the beginnings of Lia turning into the Queen that she was always meant to be. AND I ABSOLUTELY LOVED IT. She tries to protect her family, her Morrighese friends, Rafe, her new Vendan friends, her countrymen, as well as her country itself (the said country that now considers her a traitor), all while trying to survive in foreign country of “barbarians”, who all despise anything remotely resembling royalty and privilege. I loved how she defied the Komizar, at every chance she had, even though she knew that she was risking her perilous position as a prisoner every time. I also really appreciated that she didn’t allow her Morrighese upbringing to hinder her from sympathising with the Vendan people. She is such an amazing YA heroine, who didn’t wait for anyone (not even her gorgeous Prince) to save her. She was perfectly capable holding her own and standing up for herself (either with words or weapons). My only complaint about her is that she used Kaden’s feelings about her in order to manipulate him, and although I understand her reason for doing so, I still didn’t like it. :-/<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531002298ra/25939617.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
<br> <i>“And I began walking. A thousand miles, or two, I would carry her all the way to Dalbreck if I had to. No one would pry her from my arms again.”</i><br>
</blockquote><br>Ah, <b>Rafe</b>. He is exactly what every girl dreams a Prince to be. He’s kind, loyal, brave…and absolutely protective of the woman that he loves. He’d do anything to save her and I thought that their connection was so beautiful. Also, his friends were amazing, as well. I especially loved how these <i>trained soldiers</i> from Dalbreck found our young Morrighese Princess to be “scary”. HAHA! <br><br>I felt so much for <b>Kaden</b> in this novel. We learn why he has the scars on his back and my heart utterly broke for him. He was so conflicted over his emotions for Lia and his loyalty to the Komizar. The interpersonal relationships in this novel were sooo well done. Bravo! I was also shocked when we learnt that Kaden was Morrighese-born, but Vendan-raised. That certainly explains why he looks nothing like his fellow Vendans. <br><br>I found that the <b>Komizar</b> was an extremely well-written villain. He wasn’t some soulless being who went around killing everything in sight. He’s a man hungry for power, who wants to build Venda to the glory that Morrighan and Dalbrack have. He wants to give his people a better life, yet also manages to be a harsh ruler, who demands the people’s respect. Both he and Lia are very strong-willed and are worthy adversaries of each other. I found their interactions in the novel to be riveting. I’m so excited to see how Lia ultimately wins in the end. <br><br>If I had to complain about any of the characters, it would probably be <b>Pauline</b> because for someone who was so integral to the story in the previous book, she was barely in this one. I really hope that she doesn’t throw away her friendship with Lia over the discovery of Mikael being alive, but instead sees that Lia was only trying to protect her. I really hope that we see more of her in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25944798-the-beauty-of-darkness" rel="nofollow noopener">The Beauty of Darkness</a>!<br><br>This was a brilliant book that I loved from beginning to end. My issues with Pearson’s world building in The Kiss of Deception were resolved because we got the opportunity to learn SO MUCH about Venda (now, I’d like to learn more about Morrighan and Dalbreck, please!). This is a criminally underrated series that I highly recommend! &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="11511829090513874083" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/25851812-the-heart-of-betrayal">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1959224740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13199153876303984059"><b>Buddy read</b> with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/57334157-caitlin' rel='nofollow noopener'>Support Team aka Cait</a>!<br/><br/>I had high hopes going into this book since I've read several reviews stating it's way better than the first book. Was it? Yes and no. Am I disappointed? Yes. Seems like all this series does is disappoint me time and time again. I highly doubt I'm reading book 3. It's too big and I high-key lost all interest. Sad. <br/><br/>The book started off SO WELL. I was enjoying it so much and I was so glad. I've checked out a lot of reviews prior to starting the book stating th</span>
  <span id="freeText13199153876303984059" style="display:none"><b>Buddy read</b> with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/57334157-caitlin" rel="nofollow noopener">Support Team aka Cait</a>!<br /><br />I had high hopes going into this book since I've read several reviews stating it's way better than the first book. Was it? Yes and no. Am I disappointed? Yes. Seems like all this series does is disappoint me time and time again. I highly doubt I'm reading book 3. It's too big and I high-key lost all interest. Sad. <br /><br />The book started off SO WELL. I was enjoying it so much and I was so glad. I've checked out a lot of reviews prior to starting the book stating that this book is much better than the prior one and I was so happy I was feeling the exact same! Then, suddenly at around 50%, it went downhill <b>quickly</b>. Honestly, I have no idea what happened all of a sudden. I lost interest in the events, in the characters... in everything and I just couldn't wait for the book to be over. <br /><br />Like in book 1, nothing much happened in this book. It wasn't as plot-less, but I expected <i>more</i> to happen. The book had so much potential! <br /><br />Team Kaden or team Rafe? Still team Rafe. I really like Rafe! He's so sweet and lovely. Kaden's cool too but I just like Rafe way better. I still feel this series is more about the love triangle with a hint of other events here and there. I wasn't all that bothered with it in book 1 since we had the assassin/prince mystery, but here, nothing of importance was going on.<br /><br />Gotta praise Mary E. Pearson's writing. It is very addictive and easy to fly through. <br /><br />There's nothing much to say about this book other than that. OH WELL.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13199153876303984059" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=romance-pseudo-love-geometry">romance-pseudo-love-geometry</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100016974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer110948247799513383"><blockquote>
  <b>9.5 out of 10</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br/><a href='http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/07/the-heart-of-betrayal-by-mary-e-pearson.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br/><br/><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=D_3vnZqxjsU' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elaiza – I Don't Love You</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JQ_nw0lo1-k' rel='nofollow noopener'>Side Liner – Every Morning You Are My Faith</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Fiq-AC934V4' rel='nofollow noopener'>Extreme Music – Invincible</a><br/><br/><b>Genre</b>: post-apocalyptic, fantasy, YA<br/><b>Stuff</b>: any means to an end if you wanna live<br/><b>Fail</b>: first 60% are slow<br/><b>WOW</b>: final part<br/><b>POV</b>: 1st person, multi<br/><b>Love-Geometry</b>: medium<br/><br/><b>Quote-Core</b>:<blockquote> </blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText110948247799513383" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>9.5 out of 10</b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br /><a href="http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/07/the-heart-of-betrayal-by-mary-e-pearson.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br /><br /><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=D_3vnZqxjsU" rel="nofollow noopener">Elaiza – I Don't Love You</a><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JQ_nw0lo1-k" rel="nofollow noopener">Side Liner – Every Morning You Are My Faith</a><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Fiq-AC934V4" rel="nofollow noopener">Extreme Music – Invincible</a><br /><br /><b>Genre</b>: post-apocalyptic, fantasy, YA<br /><b>Stuff</b>: any means to an end if you wanna live<br /><b>Fail</b>: first 60% are slow<br /><b>WOW</b>: final part<br /><b>POV</b>: 1st person, multi<br /><b>Love-Geometry</b>: medium<br /><br /><b>Quote-Core</b>:<blockquote> “<i>Yes, royals know how to do things beyond counting our twelve toes.</i>”</blockquote><br /><b>First 50-60% of the book are just the beginning</b>: putting new characters in the plot, introduction of Venda and its specifics, alignment of forces, game planning. It wasn’t boring but my heart wasn’t pumping either. And then… I couldn’t eat, sleep, sit, stand until the book was over (and it was hard to finish the story ‘cause I was eager to know what was next and afraid of it at the same time).<br /><br /><b>So, Venda.</b> Venda’s life is quite barbaric. Indeed. And its people are narrow-minded and a bit pagandom-ish. But their traditions, language and the way they used to be aren’t worse than Morrighan’s or Darblreack’s locals have. <i>Paviamma</i>, for example, is such a beautiful word. It means love, friendship, something light, sweet and important at once. This word reminds me about Indian mantras. It’s tasty on my tongue. <br /><br /><b>Okay, what else we would know about Venda?</b><br /><br />- You can get power by killing the man whose position you desire to have. Venda has no royals. It is ruling by Komizar and his Council, governors, quarterlords and the inner guard circle named Rahtan (Kaden belongs to it).<br /><br />- Venda has no children. No matter if you’re only 5 year-old, you must work as much as adults do and your punishes would be the same as theirs. Also remember, if you die, others would come to replace you. You are replaceable. <br /><br />- Venda is located in the north. Its winters are cold and snowy. <br /><br />- The kingdom has a few lands to grow food; its territory is cut from the rest continent by a large river. Local people are doomed to die from starvation.<br /><br /><b>Lia and Rafe</b> are Komizar’s prisoners now. Komizar is 29, black-haired and black-eyed man with Christian Grey's attitude (though I think Christian can take a lesson or two from Komizar).<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    
      <b>I knew why he chose the brown. It was the plainest of my dresses, certainly drab in his eyes, but all the better to contrast and showcase the red he’d have me wear tomorrow. I had no doubt he’d ordered the snow itself as the perfect backdrop, and surely he’d ordered the sun to shine in the morning so as not to deter the crowds.</b>
    
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Lia knows that Rafe isn’t a farmer. Well, everybody knows that by now. But they have no idea that he isn’t an emissary either while Lia has. And she accepts these news without hysterics. I expected a lot of drama after this revelation, but Lia gave me a pleasant surprise. <br />He said: <br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    
      <b>I’m not the farmer I claimed to be, but I hope I can make you fall in love with me again, this time as a prince, one day at a time. We’ve had a terrible start—it doesn’t mean we can’t have a better ending.</b>
    
  </i>
</blockquote><br />And she agreed.<br /><br /><b>How Rafe convinced Komizar to keep him alive?</b> He said the King of Dalbreck is very ill and after his death the Prince would take a throne and come to Venda to make an alliance against Morrighan. Komizar believed him with one condition: if the Prince wouldn’t come in a month, his Emissary would go to Dalbreck in parts. Thank god, Rafe’s friends were already in Venda, so he hoped they would manage to sneak in the city and help him and Lia to flee. <br /><br />Kaden thought he would bring Lia in Venda and they would have happily-ever-after.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>
      Because I so stupidly loved her.
    </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Uh-huh. <b>He calls Rafe a court confectionery while he himself is a Mr. Naïve Assassin</b>. Komizar has his own plans for his girl. They start with abuse, continue with beating and end up with marriage. What's funny, Kaden isn’t a fiance. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>
      This wasn’t the story I had written for myself. Not the story of Terravin and salty breezes and love.
    </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Yes, it wasn’t. She had to escape this place. But during her time in Venda she got used to locals. They are kind but unprotected and weak, without men like Komizar they will die sooner than you think. They don't know other life. I was afraid Lia's love for them would be so big, she'd decide not to leave their country. But the terrible truth came out and she understood that not only Venda needs to be saved, the rest kingdoms are, too, in danger. <br /><br /><b>Love triangle.</b> It exists, but MC made her choice in the first book and stuck with it. Kaden loves her, but she sees in him only potential friend and a good guy among bad people. He always says that Venda comes first (until the final of the book, so now I really don’t know what would happen next) while Rafe’s priority all along was Lia and only Lia. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>
      “It was worth it, Lia,” He said. “Every mile, every day. I’d do it all again. I’d chase you across three continents if that’s what it took to be with you.”
    </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />And:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>
      “But you’re everything I want. Remember that. I love you, Lia. Not a title. And not because a piece of paper says I should. Because I do.”
    </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Isn’t it beautiful?! If Kaden would break it, I'll break him too.<br /><br />I wanna say a few words about the <b>secondary characters</b>. Pearson has lot of them in the story and each has a fate, nature and temper (no matter how much this person matters for the plot).<br /> <br />We have three kingdoms and three truths, and I ache for them all together. We know next to nothing about Darbreck but Rafe’s soldiers are good example of its locals and their are awesome.<br /><br />I can't tell much about the plot without spoilers. It was a heartbreaking journey in so many ways, but there were sweet and even hot moments among the pain. This read wasn't an easy one and the final just blew my mind. If I had a habit to gnaw my nails, my hands might be eaten too in the end of this book. <br /><br />I have some theories about the next book, but honestly, I have no idea what Mary will do or already did (I know she’s trough the 50% with <i>The Beauty of Darkness</i>). <br /><br />All I can say, I didn’t expect this book to be so good. I was ready to give it around 7-7.5 stars and then it started to get better, better and better. <br /><br /><b>PS</b>: Rafe, if Lia will end up with Kaden, you can have me. Or you can have me anyway. You’re my new book-boyfriend. Congratulations.<br /><br /><b>The Remnant Chronicles (Хроники выживших):</b><br /><blockquote>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1478773528" rel="nofollow noopener">Morrighan (Морриган)</a> #0.5/3 <br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100011566" rel="nofollow noopener">The Kiss of Deception (Поцелуи лжецов)</a> #1/3 <br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100016974" rel="nofollow noopener">The Heart of Betrayal (Сердца обманщиков)</a> #2/3 <br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1323238951" rel="nofollow noopener">The Beauty of Darkness (Прелесть тьмы)</a> #3/3</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="110948247799513383" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3306257664" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3306257664" />
    <a title="Roel ✿ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/92664725-roel"><img alt="Roel ✿ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589203115p2/92664725.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3306257664?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Roel ✿ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Roel ✿ " href="/user/show/92664725-roel">Roel ✿ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/92664725-roel?shelf=2-stars">2-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3306257664" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12539512299288985664">If this book didn't have the excellent ending it has, I would have upped and left the last book in the trilogy untouched. Lucky for me, I have decided that there is still hope for <i>The Beauty of Darkness.</i> <br/><br/><i>The Heart of Betrayal</i> continues on where the first installment left off: Lia and Rafe's arrival at the kingdom of Venda. The two get taken in as prisoners and are quickly swept up in a culture that is alien to them, getting tangled up in the leader of the kingdom's lies and manipulation in the p</span>
  <span id="freeText12539512299288985664" style="display:none">If this book didn't have the excellent ending it has, I would have upped and left the last book in the trilogy untouched. Lucky for me, I have decided that there is still hope for <i>The Beauty of Darkness.</i> <br /><br /><i>The Heart of Betrayal</i> continues on where the first installment left off: Lia and Rafe's arrival at the kingdom of Venda. The two get taken in as prisoners and are quickly swept up in a culture that is alien to them, getting tangled up in the leader of the kingdom's lies and manipulation in the process. Lia soon makes new friends, and actually starts to enjoy her new life in the 'land of barbarians'.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"Sometimes winning is not only a matter of knowing the rules, but of making your opponent think he knows them better."</b>
</i><br /><br />Now, Lia started out as a decent protagonist in book one. She made it clear that she wanted to follow her own path, she stood up for herself when she needed to, and there really wasn't ever a dull moment watching the world through her eyes. <u>In this part, I found her actions to be borderline ridiculous at times.</u> She has extreme reactions every time something doesn't go exactly the way she wants it to, her main focus in life has turned into wreaking vengeance, and she constantly makes mindless decisions that could ultimately ruin her life.<br /><br />On top of <u>losing the ability to use her brain,</u> she sometimes turns into a stone-cold, heartless person for a few scenes. She toys with Kaden's feelings and turns into her father — the very person she is trying <i>so hard</i> not to become.<br />I honestly would've loved it if Rafe and Kaden joined forces and conspired to murder Lia. They both deserve so much better!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>I shook my head. "I don't want you to think I do this a lot."<br />"Cry? Or get abducted?"<br />I smiled. "Both.”</b>
</i> <br /><br />I thought the first half of this book was charming. There were side characters that I found intriguing and nice to read about (Calantha, Aster, Griz, the Komizar) and learning more about Venda and its twisted ways and catacombs was very interesting. And again, <u>that ending.</u> It made up for the downward spiral that occurred after the first half.<br /><br />I think the main issue I have with this novel is its main characters. I don't feel connected to Lia, Rafe and Kaden at all. Looking past that, I still found the story fun and enjoyable, and the twists and turns of the plotline were well-executed!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I turned, satisfied they wouldn't be coming this way again, and went in the opposite direction. It was the first time I had twisted the gift into a sham since I'd been here, but if I wasn't going to be handed my newly earned freedoms, it appeared I would have to seize them. There were secrets just steps away that I had a right to know."</b>
</i><br /><br />---------------<br /><br /><i>Additional Notes:<br />- I have a growing distrust in GoodReads' average ratings<br />- Hopefully no die-hard Lia stans will murder me in my sleep after reading this</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12539512299288985664" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1664042629" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1664042629" />
    <a title="Hannah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38077205-hannah"><img alt="Hannah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569937560p2/38077205.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1664042629?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hannah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hannah" href="/user/show/38077205-hannah">Hannah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38077205-hannah?shelf=owned">owned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1664042629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15176818693182945342">I loved the progression of the story in this book! It definitely read more like a fantasy compared to the first book. <br/><br/>It expanded so much on the world and the mythology which was definitely my favorite part. Again, Lia's character development was amazing and I feel like we finally got to see her outside of the love triangle, which I loved. <br/><br/>I still don't like Kaden and after this book I don't think there's any redeeming him for me. But Rafe, Rafe is good.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('X+fFAIHmNmR6o1FNWBBCvKZ6XmoumhZ69QEwIYiDYKFhdB4SGxMpkbb7eDiKFYTiZP5TYl3OH1fKMBgcNild5Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zIAxOamtpJWj7+WO40S+aObXruRkFHUaq8CjZGjpiEbyE+orM1i7YG+3zPsxQXg2JFOj7BdAfDeU8YtZ1kO1Ag==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/123463.Mary_E_Pearson"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1528497378p3/123463.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6074781544062965425">Mary E. Pearson is the NYT bestselling and award-winning author of eleven YA novels and one novella. Her works include the completed trilogy, <i>The Remnant Chronicles</i>, which in a starred review, Publisher’s Weekly called <i>“masterfully crafted.”</i> Her favorite activities as a child were climbing tall trees imagining she was a hero in some fantastical world, or running along fence tops and roofs pretendi</span>
  <span id="freeText6074781544062965425" style="display:none">Mary E. Pearson is the NYT bestselling and award-winning author of eleven YA novels and one novella. Her works include the completed trilogy, <i>The Remnant Chronicles</i>, which in a starred review, Publisher’s Weekly called <i>“masterfully crafted.”</i> Her favorite activities as a child were climbing tall trees imagining she was a hero in some fantastical world, or running along fence tops and roofs pretending she was a spy with a bagful of amazing gadgets. She was rarely herself. Amazingly, she never broke a bone until she caught a basketball in gym class. Catching real balls was not her forte. These days she continues to live in make-believe worlds she creates in her books. Her latest 2-book series, <i>Dance of Thieves</i>, allows her do all kinds of dangerous things without breaking any bones. So far. <br />You can learn more about Mary and her books at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.marypearson.com">www.marypearson.com</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6074781544062965425" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
